2. **A committed intimate relationship that survives a workshop-retreat episode without rupture.** The growth event is not the relationship; it is the *first time the partner stays through the retreat and he stays through their staying.* He has never had this on the record.
3. **Mentorship at scale, formalized.** Not ad hoc protégés but a deliberate transfer-of-knowledge structure (a real institution, faculty role, foundation) in which he is *not the operator.* Forces him to tolerate other people executing his ideas imperfectly — the single skill he most lacks and which most reliably reduces his omnipotent-control activation.
4. **Therapeutic engagement with a clinician he cannot intellectually dominate.** Canon has avoided this almost entirely; the closest analogs are Bethany Cabe and the AA framework. A formal trauma-focused course (prolonged exposure for the cave; EMDR for the wormhole-class events; CBT for the catastrophizing) administered by someone immune to the charm would be transformative. He would resist; resistance is the indicator that it is working.
5. **A sustained interval of tolerated inactivity.** A month — a real month — in which he does not build anything, does not solve anything, does not optimize anything. The interoception baseline would finally be measurable. The withdrawal phenomena would be severe and informative.
6. **Grieving Howard rather than auditing him.** A discrete piece of work, possibly precipitated by becoming a parent himself (the Morgan-analog material in some continuities) or by a sponsor's direct intervention. Until this happens, the Howard-loop runs underneath every authority conflict he has.
7. **Public accountability that he does not control the framing of.** Sitting through a process — a tribunal, a truth-and-reconciliation analog — in which he is not the architect, not the explainer, not the narrator. Every prior accountability moment he has stage-managed. The growth event is the one he does not.
8. **Acceptance of being governed.** Specifically: deferring, on a substantive question on which he is right and the slower body is wrong, to the slower body, and surviving the outcome. He has never done this. It is the developmental task most directly opposite to his trauma logic, which is why it is the one most worth setting.

## 6.6 The Slow-Burn Threats — Items That Will Compound If Untreated

Distinct from the acute precipitants above; these are the chronic conditions whose unaddressed accumulation determines the floor of his functioning.

- **Sleep debt.** Cumulative across decades. The hypomanic-flavored productivity is partly defense and partly chronic dysregulation; without addressed sleep architecture, the affective lability worsens with age.
- **Cardiovascular load.** Six decades of arc-reactor-mediated cardiac function, multiple shrapnel events, stress-cardiomyopathy episode under Extremis, baseline allostatic load of his arousal level. The medical file is heavier than he carries.
- **Identity-prosthesis entanglement.** Each generation of armor sits closer to the skin. The endpoint of this trajectory — full nano-integration, neural co-residence — has psychological costs not yet measured. The question of where Tony ends and the suit begins is becoming a literal one. If the suit fails catastrophically while inside him, the somatic and psychiatric consequences would be of a kind he has no playbook for.
- **The accumulating ledger of foreseen-but-accepted costs.** Goliath. The ambassador. The Registration detentions. The Illuminati's Incursion calculus. The Inversion harms. He carries each of these as a discrete item; the cumulative weight is more than the sum, and it is not being processed at the rate it is being added to. Untreated, the ledger becomes the precipitant for a martyrdom-shaped exit at the moment a clean-looking opportunity presents.
- **The decreasing pool of peers who can challenge him.** As his cognitive ceiling stays unmatched and his accomplished peers cycle out (death, estrangement, narrative dormancy), the number of people who can tell him he is wrong shrinks. This is a structural risk independent of his psychology — it is the *epistemic* version of the relational-scaffold problem.

## 6.7 The Most Probable Five-Year Picture

Synthesizing: he will continue the Cantwell-era recovery work, with one substantive relapse-shaped event (not necessarily alcoholic — possibly a unilateral-intervention relapse) within the window, recovered from more quickly than the prior generation of such events. He will be presented with at least one Tier-2 or Tier-1 precipitant from 6.4 — most likely a Stark-tech-mediated incident or an AI-progeny crisis — and his response will be the single most diagnostic data point of the decade: whether he reaches first for the sponsor or first for the workshop. He will lose at least one element of his relational scaffold, temporarily or permanently, and the speed of his reconstitution of an equivalent will determine whether the next five-year window opens onto Fork A or Fork B. The probability of Fork C in this specific window is low but non-zero, and concentrated almost entirely in the scenario where a 6.4-Tier-1 event coincides with a scaffold loss.

## 6.8 The Single Most Important Forward Variable

If a surveillance apparatus could monitor only one signal on this subject, it would be this: **the latency between a destabilizing event and his first phone call to another human being.** Across the entire record, that latency is the leading indicator of every subsequent outcome. In 1979 and 1982 it was effectively infinite, and he lost the company twice. In Civil War it was measured in weeks, and the cost was Steve Rogers. In Disassembled it was zero in one direction (he called no one) and infinite in another (he refused everyone). In the Cantwell-era recovery work it is, for the first time on the published record, measurable in hours and sometimes minutes.

Shorten that latency and every other variable improves. Lengthen it and every other variable degrades. The forward assessment of Anthony Edward Stark, in the end, reduces to whether he picks up the phone.

## Relationship Graph
### [[Peter Benjamin Parker (Spider-Man)]]
- The kid he mentors — the son-figure he wants to do right by, offering the warmth Howard never gave him. Peter's orphan attachment and Tony's father-wound make the bond load-bearing for both, and devastating when it strains.

### [[Steve Rogers (Captain America)]]
- The Civil War rift — ideological opponents who genuinely respected and wounded each other. Tony's guilt-driven control against Steve's anti-authority conviction.

### [[Carol Danvers (Captain Marvel)]]
- The friend who, acting on precrime certainty, beat him into a coma at the end of Civil War II — the relationship destroyed by her refusal to tolerate being wrong, and the event that takes Tony off the board (and sets Doom toward the Iron Man mantle).

### Pepper Potts
- The partner who sees past the systems to the man avoiding himself with them — the relationship that calls him to the stillness he flees.
